         <div class="content">
          <header>
           <h3 class="article-name">
            RAM Benchmark Hierarchy: Fastest DDR4 Memory Kits for AMD and Intel
           </h3>
           <p class="byline">
            <span class="by-author">
             By
             <span style="white-space:nowrap">
              Zhiye Liu
             </span>
            </span>
            <time class="published-date relative-date" data-published-date="2021-03-08T21:43:56Z" datetime="2021-03-08T21:43:56Z">
            </time>
           </p>
          </header>
          <p class="synopsis">
           Our RAM benchmark hierarchy ranks memory kits of all frequencies and capacities for any budget.
          </p>
         </div>
        </article>

       <a aria-label="Doubling Down: RTX 3070 Modded with 16GB of VRAM" class="article-link" href="https://www.tomshardware.com/news/16gb-rtx-3070-mod">
        <article class="search-result search-result-news optional-image-wrapper has-rating">
         <div class="image">
          <figure class="article-lead-image-wrap" data-original="https://cdn.mos.cms.futurecdn.net/boZnVCcRU9GoQfvdjWMFsR.png">
           <div class="image-remove-flow-width-setter">
